## Phase 14.14: Track A captions-on-demand + YAML lifecycle hardening

*Shipped session 171 (Apr 28). Two adjacent concerns landed together: (a) the live-demo bug where the `claude` agent could not answer "what name did I just say" even with captions enabled, root-caused to `claude_cli.complete_streaming` only sending `messages[-1]` to its long-lived subprocess (so caption `<spoken>` blocks built up in the meeting record but never reached Claude), and (b) the brittleness of the YAML auto-import / wizard rewrite cycle that surfaced when a user-edit produced a structurally-valid YAML with a missing newline (`- Taskmcp_servers:`) and the runtime crashed eight layers down with `TypeError: '<' not supported between dict and str`.*


| Step    | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Status                                                                                                                                                               | Est.    |
| ------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------- |
| 14.14.1 | **Bundled `transcript` MCP server.** New `src/_1_800_operator/mcp_servers/transcript_server.py` (FastMCP stdio) exposing `recall_transcript(minutes_back?, last_n?)` against the meeting JSONL pointed to by `OPERATOR_MEETING_RECORD_PATH`. Filters `kind="caption"`, slices windows, returns plain-text empty-states. Registered with Claude Code via `--mcp-config <tempdir>/mcp.json` written per-spawn by `claude_cli._maybe_write_mcp_config`. Path plumbed through `LLMClient.set_record` → `provider.set_meeting_record_path`. Defense-in-depth runtime backstop appended to `--append-system-prompt` in `set_meeting_record_path` so the recall_transcript hint survives even if a user nukes ground_rules. Live-tested: spoke "Purple", asked "what color did I just say?", Claude replied "Hey Jojo — purple." 8 unit tests + handshake test. | ✅                                                                                                                                                                    | shipped |
| 14.14.2 | **Atomic YAML write.** `setup.py:_dump_yaml` rewritten to write a sibling `.tmp` file, fsync, then `os.replace` — atomic on POSIX so a crash mid-write leaves either the old or new content, never a half-written file. `__main__.py:_sync_claude_imports` routes through the same helper.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | ✅                                                                                                                                                                    | shipped |
| 14.14.3 | **Always re-import + per-entry merge.** `_bootstrap_claude_imports` (one-shot, gated on `_claude_import_done`) replaced with `_sync_claude_imports` that re-reads `~/.claude.json` + `claude mcp list` on every boot and merges per server: `command`/`args`/`env`/`auth`/`auth_url`/`description` overwritten from source, `enabled`/`hints`/`read_tools`/`confirm_tools` preserved from user, servers missing in source dropped. Stale `_claude_import_done` flag stripped on first new-format sync. Cost: ~3s `claude mcp list` shell-out every boot. 5 tests.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | ✅                                                                                                                                                                    | shipped |
| 14.14.4 | **Schema validation at config load.** `config.py` runs a hand-rolled validator after `yaml.safe_load` covering the known top-level keys (`agent`, `llm`, `transcript`, `permissions`, `skills`, `mcp_servers`, `personality`, `ground_rules`). Surfaces all violations together as a `CONFIG ERROR` block on stderr with a `operator edit <name>` next-step hint, exits 2. Catches the exact dict-instead-of-string-in-list class that bit the user this session. 10 tests.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | ✅                                                                                                                                                                    | shipped |
| 14.14.5 | **Surface MCP startup failures in chat (Track B).** `_emit_mcp_rollup` now optionally takes the connector. When any servers failed to start, posts a one-liner: *"⚠ N MCP server(s) failed to start: X. Tools from them won't work this meeting…"* Successful-only stays terminal-only (no chat clutter). 5 tests. Track A is out of scope — Claude Code manages its own MCP startup inside the subprocess.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | ✅                                                                                                                                                                    | shipped |
| 14.14.6 | `**ruamel.yaml` for round-trip preservation.** `setup.py:_load_yaml` / `_dump_yaml` and `_sync_claude_imports` now use `ruamel.yaml` round-trip mode (added as a pinned dep). User comments and `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | `block-scalar styles on`ground_rules`/`personality` survive the import-rewrite cycle. Verified end-to-end with a mixed comments/block-scalar/inline-comment fixture. | ✅       |
| 14.14.7 | `**operator edit` UX.** `_run_edit` now prints `Saved <path>` and returns 0 on editor close, instead of leaking vim's nonzero exit codes (which surfaced as a confusing red X in the user's prompt even when the file saved cleanly). Returns 1 only if the file no longer exists.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | ✅                                                                                                                                                                    | shipped |
| 14.14.8 | **Docs.** `CLAUDE.md` gained an "Imported MCP Servers — cwd & Secrets Contract" section: imported MCPs spawn from `$HOME` (use absolute paths, not relative `./` ones), put secrets in `~/.operator/.env` referenced via `${VAR}`, and the field-ownership split across re-imports. The `agents/claude/config.yaml` `ground_rules` lost the `<spoken>` line (replaced with one pointing Claude at `recall_transcript` + usage hints).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | ✅                                                                                                                                                                    | shipped |


**Phase total: shipped in one session (~3h elapsed including live-test).**

***Resolved open questions from earlier phases:***

- *Phase 14.12 open question #4 (captions in track A): resolved — captions feed the meeting JSONL same as before, but track-A's claude_cli no longer sees `<spoken>` blocks in the prompt; instead inner-claude calls the bundled `recall_transcript` MCP tool on demand.*

***Deferred (not blocking launch, surface only if real users hit them):***

- *Hash-based fast-path for the per-boot `claude mcp list` cost (~3s) if measured to matter. Now ~6s after Phase 14.15 added a second shell-out for health surface — same fast-path would cover both calls.*
- *Path-rewriting at import time for relative `command`/`args` paths in `~/.claude.json` (cwd contract documented instead — punt to user fix if it bites).*
- *Secret-shaped value detection in imported `env` blocks (decided: user's responsibility per the cwd & secrets contract).*

## Phase 14.15: Live-validation follow-ups + project-scope parity

*Shipped session 172 (Apr 28). Live-validation of session 171's Phase 14.14 work surfaced bugs and a v1 launch concern; this phase catches them before the rebrand.*


| Step    | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Status | Est.    |
| ------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ------ | ------- |
| 14.15.1 | **Project-scope MCP discovery.** `extract_imported_mcps` only walked `~/.claude.json#mcpServers` (user-scope); project-scope entries at `~/.claude.json#projects.<cwd>.mcpServers` were silently dropped. `claude mcp add` defaults to project scope, so user-added MCPs never reached operator (Sentry was missed in the wild). New `_collect_mcp_servers_from_cfg(cfg, cwd)` merges both scopes (project wins on collision); cwd is injectable for testability. 2 tests.                                   | ✅      | shipped |
| 14.15.2 | `**(HTTP)` annotation in `claude mcp list` regex.** Original regex required `URL\s+-\s+status` immediately after the URL, but claude-code prints `URL (HTTP) - status` for HTTP-not-SSE entries — silently dropping them. Added optional `(?:\s+\([A-Z]+\))?` group. 1 test.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | ✅      | shipped |
| 14.15.3 | **Project-scope skills walk.** `load_skills` gained an optional `cwd` param (defaults to `Path.cwd()`); walks `<cwd>/.claude/skills/` implicitly so Claude Code's project-scoped skills surface without needing a config edit. Mirrors the cwd-aware MCP walk. Project scope wins on name collision (last-wins after shared library + external paths). 2 tests.                                                                                                                                              | ✅      | shipped |
| 14.15.4 | **Project-scope CLAUDE.md walk.** `read_user_claude_md(cwd)` now reads `<cwd>/CLAUDE.md` and `<cwd>/.claude/CLAUDE.md` in addition to `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md`. Single-source returns bare content (preserves old wizard contract); multi-source includes section headers per source. Wizard-time only — runtime is unaffected because the inner claude subprocess does its own native CLAUDE.md discovery via `cwd=os.getcwd()`. 2 tests.                                                                      | ✅      | shipped |
| 14.15.5 | **Track A pre-flight MCP health surface.** New `discover_mcp_health()` parses `claude mcp list` for status (✓ Connected, ! Needs authentication, ✗ Failed to connect). `_sync_claude_imports` prints one stderr line per unhealthy entry: `[claude] ⚠ MCP needs attention: <name> — <status>`. Closes the v1 launch concern about Track A failures being invisible because they happen inside the inner-claude subprocess. Stderr-only (a1) with raw status (b1) per the surgical scoping decision. 2 tests. | ✅      | shipped |


**Phase total: shipped session 172 with `e174eb3` (5 source/test files, +297/-16 lines, 37/37 + skills suite all pass).**

***Deferred (still open):***

- *Session 171 order-of-operations: per-entry merge + atomic write fires BEFORE schema validation. When pre-existing corruption survives the merge (e.g. malformed `permissions.always_ask`), the user ends up with a doubly-broken file (original corruption + new clean block appended). Fix order should be: parse → validate raw → merge → validate post-merge → write. Caught while live-testing.*

## Phase 15.11: Community & Support Infrastructure ✅ SHIPPED session 189

*Set up the surfaces users will reach for when something breaks, before flipping the repo public. Non-technical work but launch-blocking — silence kills early-stage OSS faster than bugs do.*

**Why this is a dedicated phase, not a bullet inside 16.1:** The first 10 issues set the tone for whether the project feels alive or abandoned. Issue templates, labels, a `SUPPORT.md`, and notification routing all need to exist *before* the first real user files anything — they're not nice-to-haves you bolt on after.

**Decisions locked from session 187 discussion:** GitHub Issues + GitHub Discussions only at v0.0.1; no Discord, no Slack. Discord revisited at ~50 active users *if* users ask for it. PostHog/Sentry skipped at launch (privacy positioning conflict + small N makes telemetry value low; revisit Sentry crash-only opt-in post-50 users).


| Step     | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Status | Est. |
| -------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------ | ---- |
| 15.11.1  | **Enable GitHub Issues + Discussions on `1-800-operator/operator`.** Issues already on by default; turn on Discussions explicitly via repo Settings → Features. Set up Discussions categories: "Q&A", "Show & tell", "Ideas", "General".                                                                                                                                                                  | ✅      | ~10m |
| 15.11.2  | **Issue template — Bug Report.** `.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/bug_report.yml` (form-style, not free-text). Required fields: OS + version, Python version, install method (curl|sh vs git clone vs `uv tool install`), `operator --version`, command run, expected vs actual, relevant section of `/tmp/operator.log` (with redaction reminder), MCP servers enabled. Pre-filled labels: `bug`, `needs-triage`. | ✅      | ~30m |

Pre-filled labels: `enhancement`, `needs-triage`.                                                                                                                                                                   | ✅      | ~15m |

Forces users into the right channel.                                                                                                                                                                       | ✅      | ~5m  |
| 15.11.5  | `**SUPPORT.md`** at repo root — three sections: bugs → Issues, questions → Discussions, security → SECURITY.md. ~10 lines.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | ✅      | ~15m |

Triage queue weekly on Sundays." Set a recurring calendar reminder.                                                                                                                                                                            | ✅      | ~10m |

***Deferred (post-launch, gated on user signal):***

- *Discord server. Add when (a) multiple users ask "is there a Discord?", and (b) at least one power user volunteers to help moderate. Empty Discord is worse than no Discord.*
- *Sentry crash reporting (opt-in via `OPERATOR_TELEMETRY=1`, crash-only, with PII scrubbing). Revisit at ~50 active users.*
- *PostHog product analytics. Probably never on the OSS CLI; native habitat is operator-cloud.*
- *Contributor onboarding (`CONTRIBUTING.md`, dev environment setup, `good-first-issue` curation). Add when first external contributor shows up.*
- *Issue triage automation (stale-bot, auto-label by area, etc.). Wait until queue volume justifies it — under 20 open issues, do it by hand.*

## Phase 17: Upstream Drift Monitoring

*First post-MVP priority. Detect silent breakage from upstream changes (model deprecations, MCP tool schema drift, DOM changes, dep bumps) before users hit them in a live meeting.*

**Why:** The product sits on top of many moving surfaces we don't control — LLM APIs, hosted MCP servers, pinned binaries, Google Meet DOM, Playwright/Chromium, virtual audio stack, OS APIs. Nothing currently watches any of them. Failures only surface mid-meeting.


| Step | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Est. |
| ---- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ---- |
| 17.1 | Automated diff checks (weekly cron, opens GitHub issue on diff): (a) OpenAI + Anthropic model-list endpoints vs. configured models; (b) `list_tools()` schema snapshot diff per configured MCP server (catches hosted Linear/Gmail/Calendar changes + local GitHub binary drift); (c) GitHub releases for pinned MCP binaries (GitHub MCP `v0.32.0`, `mcp-remote`); (d) `pip list --outdated` filtered to critical deps (openai, anthropic, playwright, faster-whisper, mlx-whisper, rumps, kokoro); (e) Python + macOS EOL date reminders | ~3h  |
| 17.2 | Weekly smoke canary — headless run joins a test Meet, sends a chat message, invokes one read tool per configured MCP server, asserts success. Single pass catches Meet UI drift, OAuth expiry, hosted MCP outages, BlackHole/mpv regressions, Playwright/Chromium bumps                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | ~2h  |
| 17.3 | Manual checkpoint runbook — quarterly ~15min checklist for fuzzy surfaces not amenable to automation: Google Meet / OpenAI / GitHub / Linear ToS pages, Meet UI walkthrough, macOS version compatibility, kext/codesigning requirements, Kokoro model repo status                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | ~1h  |


**Phase total: ~6h**

---

## Post-MVP

*Everything below was scoped out of the 7-day MVP window. Prioritize based on user feedback after launch.*

### Gate `operator dial` behind the plugin (deprecate terminal entry)

**Origin: Session 224 (2026-05-13).** Today's debugging surfaced the state-scan footgun: when `operator dial` runs from a terminal without `--resume-session` and without `CLAUDE_CODE_SESSION_ID`, operator falls through to "state-scan" — grabbing the most recently modified entry out of the desktop app's `claude-code-sessions/` catalog. That catalog can desync from the CLI's actual conversation store (claude returns "No conversation found with session ID: …"), and operator's auto-retry re-uses the same stale id and also fails. The slash-command flow doesn't have this problem because it always passes a live `--resume-session <id>`.

**Proposal:** delete the bare `operator dial` terminal entry point. The slash command becomes the only way to enter a meeting. State-scan and `_discover_session_from_claude_state` become dead code and get deleted with it. Audio-debug toggle moves off `OPERATOR_AUDIO_DEBUG=1` env-var prefix onto a file marker (e.g. `~/.operator/.audio_debug`) so the slash-command flow can use it.

**Why post-MVP:** ergonomics; helpful for the imminent debugging cycle to keep both entry points available. Deferred until current chat-panel / audio-attribution work stabilizes.

### MCP Enhancements


| Item                                                  | Origin                   | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| ----------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Meeting-history MCP + skill                           | session 161 (2026-04-25) | Build a local MCP server that exposes the per-meeting JSONL at `~/.operator/history/<slug>.jsonl` as searchable/queryable history (e.g. `search_transcript`, `get_window(start, end)`, `summarize_speaker(name)`), plus a bundled skill that teaches the bot when to call it. Goal: stop carrying the rolling caption tail in the system prompt at all — the LLM pulls only the slice it needs, on demand, when asked about earlier in a long meeting. Removes the `llm.history_messages` cap as a context-window pressure point and lets a 1-hour meeting be referenced without prompt bloat. Pairs with skill frontmatter `mcp-required: [meeting-history]` so the wizard locks the toggle on.                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| Mid-meeting brain reset for `claude` / `codex` agents | session 180 (2026-05-02) | Today, both presets read their MCPs (`~/.claude.json` / `~/.codex/config.toml`) and skills (`~/.claude/skills/` / `~/.codex/skills/`) when their CLI subprocess starts. If the bot installs a new skill or MCP mid-meeting (e.g. via codex's bundled `skill-installer`, or `claude mcp add ...`), the new tool isn't actually usable until the *next* meeting because the brain process is already running. Add a `@bot reset` chat command (and matching internal hook) that gracefully tears down the brain subprocess, respawns it, and resumes the chat loop without making the user leave and re-join. Needs: idempotent shutdown of the brain MCP entry, transparent state handoff (`MeetingRecord` already persists chat tail), and a "reset complete — try again?" reply pattern. Pairs naturally with the wizard guidance line that points users at global codex/claude commands for installing tools. |
| Configurable confirmation modes                       | 10.2 (original)          | Full 4-mode system: `auto-all`, `read-auto`, `confirm-all`, `session-trust` + `batch_preview` toggle                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Read-only tool classification engine                  | 10.3 (original)          | Auto-classify tools as read/write from descriptions at discovery time                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Managed MCP client layer                              | 10.6                     | Point at an MCP proxy/gateway (Cloudflare, etc.) instead of local stdio servers                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Pin MCP server versions                               | 10.7                     | Lock `mcp-remote` and GitHub binary to specific versions in config                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| MCP server CI health check                            | 10.8 (original)          | CI job that starts servers + dry-run tool calls, alert on failure                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Runtime failure monitoring dashboard                  | 10.9 (original)          | Per-server failure rate tracking, threshold alerts, diagnostics surface                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Idempotency guards                                    | 10.10                    | Detect duplicate tool actions from repeated requests; dedup logic beyond write confirmation                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Parallel tool calls                                   | 11.2                     | Currently disabled on both providers (`parallel_tool_calls=False` on OpenAI, `disable_parallel_tool_use=True` on Anthropic) so the one-tool-at-a-time loop in `LLMClient.ask()` stays safe. Re-enable for skills that fan out across MCP servers (e.g. "what's on my plate across Linear + GitHub?"). Requires `LLMClient` to execute N tool_calls per turn and feed back N tool_results before the next LLM turn.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Per-meeting voice toggle                              | session 169 (2026-04-26) | `agent.voice: plain                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| Self-correcting MCP-hint loop                         | session 204 (2026-05-06) | Instruct the in-meeting model to log every reply where its MCP usage produced an undesirable answer (wrong scope, wrong filter, wrong tool pick — e.g. an org-wide Sentry `is:unresolved` query that hid issues outside the user's "My Projects" filter, where project-scoping would have surfaced them). On each occurrence the bot acknowledges the miss in chat and offers to write a short, durable hint attached to the offending tool/MCP so the next call self-corrects. Hints accumulate in a per-user store the brain reads alongside its tool descriptions at spawn (similar shape to the auto-memory `feedback_*` files). Goal: the bot gets sharper at each user's MCP setup over time without the user having to hand-author tool docs. Open design questions: where the hint store lives (likely under `~/.operator/hints/`), how hints are scoped (per-tool vs per-server vs per-(tool,user-intent)), and how stale hints are pruned. Pairs naturally with the mid-meeting brain-reset entry above (a fresh hint takes effect at the next reset, not the next meeting).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
